## Diagram 2

```mermaid
flowchart LR
  PhotoViewer[PhotoViewer Component] --> ModalModal[Modal (size: xl, backdrop: static)]
  ModalModal --> ModalHeader[Modal.Header: title, closeButton]
  ModalModal --> ModalBody[Modal.Body]
  ModalBody --> AlertComp[Alert (alertVariant)]
  ModalBody --> Layout[Flex Column]
  Layout --> LeftPane[Left (25%)]
  Layout --> RightPane[Right (75%)]
  LeftPane --> CategoryListComp[CategoryList]
  RightPane --> MaybeEditor{photoCategories[categoryIndex].isEditable?}

  MaybeEditor -->|false| NoEditor[No Editor]
  RightPane --> Scroll[SimpleBar]

  PhotoViewer --> SaveChangesModalComp[SaveChangesModal (global)]
```

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
  [*] --> Hidden
  Hidden --> Shown: setShow(true)
  Shown --> Loading: show && fetchPhotoData(vinId, submissionId)
  Loading --> Ready: currentLoadStatus == "success"
  Loading --> Failed: currentLoadStatus == "failed"
  Ready --> Editing: photoCategories[categoryIndex]?.isEditable
  Editing --> SaveModalShown: setShowSaveModal(true)
  SaveModalShown --> Confirmed: submitData()
  Confirmed --> Loading: submitData triggers updateData
  Editing --> Discarding: resetImageList()
  Discarding --> Ready: previewFiles cleared
  Failed --> Ready: retry / setShow(false) or fetchPhotoData retry
  Shown --> Hidden: hideHandler()
```
